<span id="freeTextContainer304450291611811326"><br/>Great 2nd book!<br/>Sexy, exciting, frustrating, heartbreaking.<br/>4.5 Stars only because of all that horrible religious talk and the overuse of the word PLEASE ☺<br/>And of course it's all so very ridiculous. The whole book could be 200 pages shorter if they didn't repeat every argument a thousand times! It's all way too naive and stupid. Just talk to each other or just don't start the relationship at all - they could've waited five weeks!?!? Ugh. So many things that are stupid in these books - BUT I still l</span>
  <span id="freeText304450291611811326" style="display:none"><br>Great 2nd book!<br>Sexy, exciting, frustrating, heartbreaking.<br>4.5 Stars only because of all that horrible religious talk and the overuse of the word PLEASE ☺<br>And of course it's all so very ridiculous. The whole book could be 200 pages shorter if they didn't repeat every argument a thousand times! It's all way too naive and stupid. Just talk to each other or just don't start the relationship at all - they could've waited five weeks!?!? Ugh. //<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('FYbuET7nhkIBBI7OALjEUD0kwYUnn9KWR7n68dO/D5YvoIfDhblPKqYvOq/3Tc6P63smTekSXPEcx7xAHvz9DA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('GaZ293TcS9KWrB+0CqUIZ6+8guLiWL848wAb4N66xwkjgB8lz4KCujGHq9X9UAK4eeNlKizVMV+ofl1RE/k1kw==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<span id="freeTextContainer15746841124830386056">"Gabriel's Promise" has been released and is now available across platforms: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://amzn.to/2Y6ah10'>https://amzn.to/2Y6ah10</a><br/><br/>My New York Times Best Selling Gabriel Series has been acquired by Passionflix. "Gabriel's Inferno" is available now on Passionflix.com. "Gabriel's Rapture" will resume filming in 2021. You can meet the cast, read the most recent update, and learn how to sign up for Passionflix here: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://sylvainreynard.com/film-series-news/'>http://sylvainr</a></span>
  <span id="freeText15746841124830386056" style="display:none">"Gabriel's Promise" has been released and is now available across platforms: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://amzn.to/2Y6ah10">https://amzn.to/2Y6ah10</a><br /><br />My New York Times Best Selling Gabriel Series has been acquired by Passionflix. "Gabriel's Inferno" is available now on Passionflix.com. "Gabriel's Rapture" will resume filming in 2021. You can meet the cast, read the most recent update, and learn how to sign up for Passionflix here: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://sylvainreynard.com/film-series-news/">http://sylvainreynard.com/film-series...</a><br /><br />You can view the trailer to the third and final part here: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=mjPUGem9SaY">https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=mjPUG...</a><br /><br />Huffington Post Books ranked "Gabriel's Inferno" as the best teacher/student romance novel. <br /><br />My latest book, "The Man in the Black Suit, (#TMitBS), is a contemporary romance/suspense standalone novel, set in Paris: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://t.co/pdpHlvVtjO">https://t.co/pdpHlvVtjO</a><br /><br />The Florentine Series is now complete. Each paperback edition has additional content. Audio and ebooks are also available.<br /><br />The second book in that series, "The Raven," was nominated by RT Magazine as Best Paranormal Romance Suspense novel of 2015.<br /><br />I am honoured to have had my novels appear on the New York Times and USAToday Bestseller lists. <br /><br />I was a Semifinalist for Best Author in the 2011 and 2012 Goodreads Choice Awards. "Gabriel's Inferno" was a Semifinalist for Best Romance in 2011 and "Gabriel's Rapture" was a Finalist for Best Romance in 2012, in the Goodreads Choice Awards, as well. The final novel in The Gabriel Series, "Gabriel's Redemption," debuted at #6 on the New York Times Bestseller list. It was a Finalist for a 2014 Goodreads Choice Award as Best Romance.<br /><br />I'm interested in the way literature can help us explore aspects of the human condition - particularly suffering, sex, love, faith, and redemption. My favourite stories are those in which a character takes a journey, either a physical journey to a new and exciting place, or a personal journey in which he or she learns something about himself/herself. <br /><br />I'm also interested in how aesthetic elements such as art, architecture, food, drink, and music can be used to tell a story or to illuminate the traits of a particular character. In my writing, I combine all of these elements with the themes of redemption, forgiveness, and the transformative power of goodness.<br /><br />I try to use my platform as an author to raise awareness about the following charities: Now I Lay Me Down to Sleep Foundation, WorldVision, Alex's Lemonade Stand, and Covenant House. <br /><br />For more information, see my Twitter account or my website.<br /><br />I also do not check my Goodreads email.<br /><br />To email me, please use the below addy. <br />info@sylvainreynard.com</span>
